###########################
# Spanish Events
###########################

add_namespace = spain
add_namespace = spain_diplo
add_namespace = spain_elections
add_namespace = debugspain
add_namespace = spain_celections
add_namespace = spain_news


#load the whole fucking tree
country_event = {
	id = debugspain.1
	title = debugspain.1.t
	desc = debugspain.1
	picture = x
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	option = {
		name = debugspain.1.o1
		set_country_flag = spr_show_the_whole_damn_tree
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
	}
}
#make the coups run on time
country_event = {
	id = debugspain.2
	title = debugspain.2.t
	desc = debugspain.2
	picture = x
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes
	
	option = {
		name = debugspain.2.o1
		IF = { #republican coup
			limit = {
				has_stability < 0.5
				check_variable = {
					var = military_anger
					value = 8
					compare = less_than
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = spain.32
			}
		}
		IF = { #felipe stays
			limit = {
				has_stability > 0.5
				check_variable = {
					var = military_anger
					value = 8
					compare = less_than
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = spain.33
			}
		}
		IF = { #military coup
			limit = {
				has_stability > 0.5
				check_variable = {
					var = military_anger
					value = 8
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = spain.34
			}
		}
		IF = { #civil war
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = spanish_crisis_over
				has_stability < 0.5
				check_variable = {
					var = military_anger
					value = 8
					compare = greater_than_or_equals
				}
			}
			country_event = {
				id = spain.35
			}
		}
	}
}

#juan carlos sick
country_event = {
	id = spain.1
	title = spain.1.t
	desc = spain.1.d
	picture = spr_carlos_not_feeling_good

	trigger = {
		original_tag = SPR
		date > 2010.1.25
	}

	fire_only_once = yes

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 7
	}

	option = {
		name = spain.1.a
		hidden_effect = {
		    SPR = {
		        country_event = { days = 26 id = spain.2 }
				country_event = { days = 34 id = spain.5 }
				country_event = { days = 37 id = spain.8 }
				country_event = { days = 39 id = spain.9 }
				country_event = { days = 46 id = spain.10 }
				country_event = { days = 60 id = spain.13 }
				country_event = { days = 67 id = spain.16 }
				country_event = { days = 81 id = spain.19 }
				country_event = { days = 88 id = spain.20 }
				country_event = { days = 95 id = spain.23 }
				country_event = { days = 98 id = spain.26 }
				country_event = { days = 102 id = spain.29 }
				set_variable = {military_anger = 0}
		    }
		}
	}
}

	desc = spain.2.d
	picture = spr_carlos_heart_attack

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = spain.2.a
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				days = 1
				id = spain.3
			}
		}
	}
}
#carlos dead
country_event = {
	id = spain.3
	title = spain.3.t
	desc = spain.3.d
	picture = spr_carlos_fucking_dies

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = spain.3.a
		kill_country_leader = yes
		create_country_leader = {
			 name = "Felipe VI"
			 picture = Portrait_SPR_Felipe_VI.dds
			 ideology = absolute_monarchist
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				days = 1
				id = spain.4
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							tag = SPR
							tag = SPN
						}
					}
				}
				news_event = {
					id = spain_news.3
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

		name = spain.5.a
		ai_chance = { base = 25 }
		add_political_power = -150
		add_stability = 0.02
		hidden_effect = {
			SPR = {
				country_event = { days = 1 id = spain.6 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = spain.5.b
		ai_chance = { base = 75 }
		add_stability = -0.02
		hidden_effect = {
			SPR = {
				country_event = { days = 1 id = spain.7 }
			}
		}
	}
}

#ETA demands Basque Independence
country_event = {
	id = spain.20
	title = spain.20.t
	desc = spain.20.d
	picture = spr_eta_demands_basque_independence

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = spain.20.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 35
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = SPA_ai_behavior_civwar_rw
						option = SPR_CIVIL_WAR_REGIONALIST
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = SPA_ai_behavior_civwar_rw
						option = SPR_CIVIL_WAR_REPUBLICAN_REGIONALIST
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = SPA_ai_behavior_civwar_rw
						option = SPR_CIVIL_WAR_INDEPENDENCE
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = SPA_ai_behavior_civwar_rw
						option = SPR_CIVIL_WAR_INDEPENDENCE_REPUBLICAN
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = spain_military_anger_2_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			SPR = {
				add_to_variable = { military_anger = 2 }
				country_event = { days = 1 id = spain.21 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = spain.20.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 65
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = SPA_ai_behavior_civwar_rw
						option = SPR_CIVIL_WAR_AVOIDED
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = SPA_ai_behavior_civwar_rw
						option = SPR_CIVIL_WAR_REPUBLICAN
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
		hidden_effect = {
			SPR = {
				country_event = { days = 1 id = spain.22 }
			}
		}
	}
}
#Basques given autonomy
country_event = {
	id = spain.21
	title = spain.21.t
	desc = spain.21.d
	picture = spr_felipe_makes_basque_autonomy

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = spain.21.a
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = BSQ
			}
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = autonomous_state }
		}
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = idea_SPR_separatist_woes_start
			add_idea = idea_SPR_separatist_woes_basques_appeased
		}
	}
}
#fought the basques

}

#Galicians given autonomy
country_event = {
	id = spain.27
	title = spain.27.t
	desc = spain.27.d
	picture = spr_felipe_makes_galician_autonomy

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = spain.27.a
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = GAL
			}
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = autonomous_state }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {has_idea = idea_SPR_separatist_woes_basques_appeased}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = idea_SPR_separatist_woes_basques_appeased
					add_idea = idea_SPR_separatist_woes_basques_and_galicians_appeased
				}
			}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = idea_SPR_separatist_woes_basques_worse_rest_norm
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = idea_SPR_separatist_woes_basques_worse_rest_norm
				add_idea = idea_SPR_separatist_woes_basques_bad_galicians_good
			}
		}
	}
}
#fought the Galicians
country_event = {
	id = spain.28
	title = spain.28.t
	desc = spain.28.d
	picture = spr_galician_nationalists_gain_support

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = spain.28.a
		set_country_flag = GAL_will_revolt
		if = {
			limit = {has_idea = idea_SPR_separatist_woes_basques_appeased}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = idea_SPR_separatist_woes_basques_appeased
					add_idea = idea_SPR_separatist_woes_basques_good_galicians_bad
				}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {has_idea = idea_SPR_separatist_woes_basques_worse_rest_norm}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = idea_SPR_separatist_woes_basques_worse_rest_norm
					add_idea = idea_SPR_separatist_woes_basques_bad_galicians_bad
				}
		}
	}
}
#Catalonia demands autonomy
country_event = {
	id = spain.29
	title = spain.29.t
	desc = spain.29.d
	picture = spr_catalonia_demands_independence

	is_triggered_only = yes

		option = { #grant independence
		name = spain.29.a
		ai_chance = {
			base = 35
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = SPA_ai_behavior_civwar_rw
						option = SPR_CIVIL_WAR_REGIONALIST
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = SPA_ai_behavior_civwar_rw
						option = SPR_CIVIL_WAR_REPUBLICAN_REGIONALIST
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = SPA_ai_behavior_civwar_rw
						option = SPR_CIVIL_WAR_INDEPENDENCE
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = SPA_ai_behavior_civwar_rw
						option = SPR_CIVIL_WAR_INDEPENDENCE_REPUBLICAN
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		add_stability = 0.02
		custom_effect_tooltip = spain_military_anger_5_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			SPR = {
			add_to_variable = { military_anger = 5 }
			country_event = { days = 1 id = spain.30 }
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #send in the troops
		name = spain.29.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 65

					has_game_rule = {

						rule = SPA_ai_behavior_civwar_rw

#Catalans given autonomy
country_event = {
	id = spain.30
	title = spain.30.t
	desc = spain.30.d
	picture = spr_felipe_makes_catalan_autonomy

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = spain.30.a
		set_country_flag = spanish_crisis_over
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = CAT
			}
			add_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = autonomous_state }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {has_idea = idea_SPR_separatist_woes_basques_good_galicians_bad}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = idea_SPR_separatist_woes_basques_good_galicians_bad
				add_idea = idea_SPR_separatist_woes_basques_good_galicians_bad_catalans_good
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {has_idea = idea_SPR_separatist_woes_basques_bad_galicians_bad}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = idea_SPR_separatist_woes_basques_bad_galicians_bad
				add_idea = idea_SPR_separatist_woes_basques_bad_galicians_bad_catalans_good
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {has_idea = idea_SPR_separatist_woes_basques_bad_galicians_good}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = idea_SPR_separatist_woes_basques_bad_galicians_good
				add_idea = idea_SPR_separatist_woes_basques_bad_galicians_good_catalans_good
			}
		}
		else = {
			remove_ideas = {idea_SPR_separatist_woes_basques_and_galicians_appeased }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = debugspain.2
				days = 3
			}
		}
	}
}
#fought the Catalans
country_event = {
	id = spain.31
	title = spain.31.t
	desc = spain.31.d
	picture = spr_puigdemont_returns_to_catalonia

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = spain.31.a
		hidden_effect = {
			SPR = {
				country_event = { days = 1 id = spain.36 }
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			IF = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = felipe_youth
				}
				SPR = {
					country_event = {
						id = spain.235
						days = 14
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#republican coup
country_event = {
	id = spain.32
	title = spain.32.t
	desc = spain.32.d
	picture = spr_republicans_storm_the_palace

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	option = {
		name = spain.32.a
		remove_ideas = {idea_SPR_subversives_organizing}
		set_cosmetic_tag = SPR_Rep
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = revolutionary_socialist
			popularity = 0.21
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communist
			popularity = 0.24
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = moderate_socialist
			popularity = 0.12
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = new_democrat
			popularity = 0.10
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = liberal
			popularity = 0.05
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = monarchist
			popularity = -0.15
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = moderate_socialist
			elections_allowed = no
			last_election = "1935.12.17"
			election_frequency = 48
		}
		set_country_flag = republican_coup
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		set_variable = {military_anger = 0}
		add_ideas = {idea_SPR_lingering_military_radicalism}
		complete_national_focus = SPR_republican_coup
		hidden_effect = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = SPR_Rep
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_ideas = spr_sic_ione_belarra
			add_ideas = spr_fom_juan_lopez_de_uralde
			add_ideas = spr_ind_anton_gomez_reino
			add_ideas = spr_nsm_teresa_rodriguez
			add_ideas = spr_inm_inigo_errejon
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = spain_republican_coup_ministers_tooltip
		custom_effect_tooltip = SPR_you_can_train_and_edit_now
		hidden_effect = {
			country_lock_all_division_template = no
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							tag = SPR
							tag = SPN
						}
					}
				}
				news_event = {
					id = spain_news.9
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#military coup
country_event = {
	id = spain.34
	title = spain.34.t
	desc = spain.34.d
	picture = spr_military_deposes_felipe

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}
	option = {
		name = spain.34.a
		remove_ideas = {idea_SPR_subversives_organizing}
		set_country_flag = spanish_crisis_over
		set_country_flag = military_coup
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = fascist
			long_name = SPR_Military_Administration_long
			name = SPR_Military_Administration
		}
		create_country_leader = {
			 name = "Fulgencio Coll Bucher"
			 picture = Portrait_SPR_Fulgencio_Coll_Bucher.dds
			 ideology = francoist
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = fascist
			elections_allowed = no
			last_election = "1935.12.17"
			election_frequency = 48
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = nationalist
			popularity = 0.06
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascist
			popularity = 0.20
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_bolshevik
			popularity = 0.15
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = monarchist
			popularity = -0.10
		}
		set_variable = {military_anger = 0}
		complete_national_focus = SPR_military_coup
		add_ideas = {
			idea_SPR_general_strike
			idea_SPR_lingering_republican_radicalism
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = SPR_you_can_train_and_edit_now
		hidden_effect = {
			country_lock_all_division_template = no
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						OR = {
								tag = SPR
							tag = SPN
						}
					}
				}
				news_event = {
					id = spain_news.8
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

						logistics_skill=3
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = train_equipment
						amount = 50
					}
				}
				SPR = {
					CAT = {
						transfer_technology = yes
					}
				}
				SPR = {
					IF = {
						limit = {has_country_flag = BSQ_will_revolt}
						country_event = { days = 1 id = spain.37 }
						}
					IF = {
						limit = {has_country_flag = GAL_will_revolt}
						country_event = { days = 14 id = spain.38 }
					}
					IF = {
						limit = {has_country_flag = CAT_real_mad}
						CAT = {load_oob = CAT_Extra}
					}
					retire_character = SPR_Rafael_Comas
					retire_character = SPR_Miguel_Angel_Villarroya
				}
			}
		SPR = {
			declare_war_on = { target = CAT type = annex_everything }
		}
	}
	option = {    #catalonia
		name = spain.36.b
		set_country_flag = catalan_war
		remove_ideas = {idea_SPR_subversives_organizing}

		CAT = {
			transfer_state = 165
			transfer_state = 911
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = {
					id = cat.18
					days = 2
				}
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = CAT
			}
			remove_core_of = ROOT
		}
		CAT = {
            change_tag_from = SPR
        }
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = spain.177
				days = 120
			}
			news_event = {
				id = spain_news.10
			}
		}
		SPR = {
			declare_war_on = { target = CAT type = annex_everything }
			hidden_effect = {
				country_lock_all_division_template = no
			}
		}
        hidden_effect = {
			CAT = {load_oob = CAT_Revolution}
		    SPR = {
			    CAT = { transfer_technology = yes }

		    }
			SPR = {
				IF = {
					limit = {has_country_flag = BSQ_will_revolt}
					country_event = { days = 1 id = spain.37 }
					}
				IF = {
					limit = {has_country_flag = GAL_will_revolt}
					country_event = { days = 1 id = spain.38 }
				}
				IF = {
					limit = {has_country_flag = CAT_real_mad}
					CAT = {load_oob = CAT_Extra}
				}
			}
			CAT = {
				add_field_marshal_role = {
					Character = CAT_Miguel_Angel_Villarroya
					traits={ politically_connected brilliant_strategist trait_cautious media_personality defensive_doctrine }
					skill=4
					attack_skill=3
					defense_skill=4
					planning_skill=3
					logistics_skill=3

					skill=2
					attack_skill=2

country_event = {
	id = spain.38
	title = spain.38.t
	desc = spain.38.d
	picture = spr_galicia_revolts

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {    #stay with spain
		name = spain.38.a
		remove_ideas = {idea_SPR_subversives_organizing}

		GAL = {
			transfer_state = 171
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				GAL = {load_oob = GAL_Revolution}
				SPR = {
					GAL = {
						transfer_technology = yes
					}
				}
				SPR = {
					IF = {
						limit = {has_country_flag = GAL_real_mad}
						GAL = {load_oob = GAL_Extra}
					}
				}
			}
		SPR = {
			declare_war_on = { target = GAL type = annex_everything }
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = SPA_ai_behavior_civwar_rw
							option = SPR_CIVIL_WAR_INDEPENDENCE
						}
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = SPA_ai_behavior_civwar_rw
							option = SPR_CIVIL_WAR_INDEPENDENCE_REPUBLICAN
						}
					}
				}
				SPR = {
					country_event = spain.39
				}
			}
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = GAL
			}
			remove_core_of = SPR
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = GAL
				}
				remove_core_of = SPN
			}
			SPR = {
				retire_character = SPR_Fernando_Lens_Astray
				retire_character = SPR_Jose_Julio_Rodriguez_Fernandez

			GAL = {
				add_corps_commander_role = {

					attack_skill=3

					type = train_equipment

				}

		}

			base = 0
		}

			}
		GAL = {
            change_tag_from = SPR
        }
		hidden_effect = {
			GAL = {load_oob = GAL_Revolution}
			SPR = {
				BSQ = {
					transfer_technology = yes
				}
			}
			SPR = {
				IF = {
					limit = {has_country_flag = GAL_real_mad}
					GAL = {load_oob = GAL_Extra}
				}
			}
		}
		SPR = {
			declare_war_on = { target = GAL type = annex_everything }
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = GAL

		}

					is_core_of = GAL

#Secessionists offer peace after stalemate
country_event = {
	id = spain.39
	title = spain.39.t
	desc = spain.39.d
	picture = spr_secessionists_offer_peace

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			tag = SPR
			tag = SPN
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = spain_gets_revenge
		}
		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = SPR_republican_coup
		}
		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = SPR_military_coup
		}
		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = SPR_felipe_stays
		}
		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = carlist_el_rey_rojo
		}
		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = stalinist_factional_deadlock
		}
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = SPR
		}
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = SPN
		}
		OR = {
			has_war_with = GAL
			has_war_with = CAT
			has_war_with = BSQ
		}
		has_country_flag = spr_separatist_war_started_120_days_ago
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}

	option = { #sign peace
		name = spain.39.a
		ai_chance = { base = 50 }
		hidden_effect = {
			white_peace = GAL
			white_peace = BSQ
			white_peace = CAT
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = CAT
			}
			CAT = {
				transfer_state = 852
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				CAT = {
					controls_state = 177
				}
			}
			CAT = {
				transfer_state = 177
			}
		}
		country_event = {days = 1 id = spain.42}
	}

	option = { #keep fighting
		name = spain.39.b
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = SPA_ai_behavior_civwar_rw
						option = SPR_CIVIL_WAR_INDEPENDENCE_REPUBLICAN
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = SPA_ai_behavior_civwar_rw
						option = SPR_CIVIL_WAR_INDEPENDENCE
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		add_stability = -0.05
		set_country_flag = spain_kept_fighting
	}
}

	title = spain.40.t
	desc = spain.40.d
	picture = spr_secessionists_offer_peace_after_taking_valencia

			controls_province = 6906

		}

			has_completed_focus = SPR_military_coup
		}
		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = SPR_felipe_stays
		}
		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = carlist_el_rey_rojo
		}

			has_completed_focus = stalinist_factional_deadlock
		}

		}

	title = spain.41.t

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = SPR
		has_country_flag = catalan_war
		has_war = no
		has_government = monarchist
	}

		days = 1
	}

	option = {
		name = spain.41.a
		set_country_flag = felipe_stays
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		add_ideas = {
			idea_SPR_general_strike
			idea_SPR_lingering_republican_radicalism
		}
	}
}
#military overthrows felipe for surrendering
country_event = {
	id = spain.42
	title = spain.42.t
	desc = spain.42.d
	picture = spr_military_deposes_felipe_for_surrendering

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = spain.42.a
		remove_ideas = {idea_SPR_subversives_organizing}
		add_ideas = {idea_SPR_general_strike}
		set_country_flag = military_coup
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = fascist
			long_name = SPR_Military_Administration_long
			name = SPR_Military_Administration
		}
		create_country_leader = {
			 name = "Fulgencio Coll Bucher"
			 picture = Portrait_SPR_Fulgencio_Coll_Bucher.dds
			 ideology = francoist
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = fascist
			elections_allowed = no
			last_election = "1935.12.17"
			election_frequency = 48
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = nationalist
			popularity = 0.06
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = fascist
			popularity = 0.20
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = national_bolshevik
			popularity = 0.15
		}
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = monarchist
			popularity = -0.10
		}
		set_variable = {military_anger = 0}
		hidden_effect = {
			IF = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_stability < 0.30
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = SPA_ai_behavior_civwar_rw
							option = SPR_CIVIL_WAR_INDEPENDENCE_REPUBLICAN
						}
					}
				}
			set_country_flag = civil_war_coming
			country_event = {days = 1 id = spain.43}
		}
			ELSE = {
				add_ideas = {idea_SPR_lingering_republican_radicalism}
			}
		}
	}
}

					}

						rule = SPA_ai_behavior_rw

		}
	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #align with far left
		name = spain.50.a
		set_country_flag = submitted_to_strikers
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		complete_national_focus = SPR_submitted_to_general_strike
		hidden_effect = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = SPR_Rep
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							tag = SPR
							tag = SPN
						}
					}
				}
				news_event = {
					id = spain_news.18
				}
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = SPA_ai_behavior_rw
						option = SPR_LEFT_COALITION
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = SPA_ai_behavior_rw
						option = SPR_RIGHT_COALITION
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = SPA_ai_behavior_rw
						option = SPR_CONSTITUTIONAL_MONARCHY
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #hold elections anyway
		name = spain.50.b
		set_country_flag = held_elections_anyway
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		complete_national_focus = SPR_continue_with_elections
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = SPA_ai_behavior_rw
						option = SPR_STALINIST
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = SPA_ai_behavior_rw
						option = SPR_LENINIST
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = SPA_ai_behavior_rw
						option = SPR_NEOCOMMUNIST
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = SPA_ai_behavior_rw
						option = SPR_SYNDICALIST
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = spain.55
	title = spain.55.t
	desc = spain.55.d
	picture = spr_commie_party_debates_begin

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {#leninist and neocom
		name = spain.55.a
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = spain.56 days = 1}
			set_variable = {
				spain_leninist_support = 1
			}
			set_variable = {
				spain_neocom_support = 1
			}
			set_variable = {
				spain_syndicalist_support = 0
			}
			set_country_flag = spr_ai_leninist_or_neocommunist
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = SPA_ai_behavior_rw
						option = SPR_SYNDICALIST
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = SPA_ai_behavior_rw
						option = SPR_STALINIST
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}
	option = {#syndicalist
		name = spain.55.b
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = spain.56 days = 1 }
			set_variable = {
				spain_leninist_support = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				spain_neocom_support = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				spain_syndicalist_support = 1
			}
			set_country_flag = spr_ai_syndicalist
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				OR = {
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = SPA_ai_behavior_rw
						option = SPR_LENINIST
					}
					has_game_rule = {
						rule = SPA_ai_behavior_rw
						option = SPR_NEOCOMMUNIST
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
	}
}
#united left debates phase 2:matter of the crown
country_event = {
	id = spain.56
	title = spain.56.t
	desc = spain.56.d
	picture = spr_commie_party_debates_part_2

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {#leninist and syndicalists
		name = spain.56.a
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = spain.57 days = 1 }
			add_to_variable = { spain_leninist_support = 1 }
			add_to_variable = { spain_syndicalist_support = 1 }
			IF = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = spr_ai_leninist_or_neocommunist
				}
				set_country_flag = spr_ai_leninist
			}
			IF = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = spr_ai_syndicalist
				}
				set_country_flag = spr_ai_syndicalist_2
			}
		}
        ai_chance = {
            base = 5
            modifier = {
                has_country_flag = spr_ai_leninist_or_neocommunist
                factor = 10
            }
            modifier = {
                has_country_flag = spr_ai_syndicalist
                factor = 19
            }
						modifier = {
							OR = {
								has_game_rule = {
									rule = SPA_ai_behavior_rw
									option = SPR_NEOCOMMUNIST
								}
								has_game_rule = {
									rule = SPA_ai_behavior_rw
									option = SPR_STALINIST
								}
							}
							factor = 0
						}
        }
	}
	option = {#neocom
		name = spain.56.b
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = { id = spain.57 days = 1 }
			add_to_variable = { spain_neocom_support = 1 }
			set_country_flag = spr_ai_neocommunist
		}
        ai_chance = {
            base = 5
            modifier = {
                has_country_flag = spr_ai_leninist_or_neocommunist
                factor = 10
            }
						modifier = {
							OR = {
								has_game_rule = {
									rule = SPA_ai_behavior_rw
									option = SPR_SYNDICALIST
								}
							}
							factor = 0
						}
        }
	}
}

#committee victor emerges
country_event = {
	id = spain.58
	title = spain.58.t
	picture = spr_united_left_debates_end
	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	desc = { #leninist victory
		text = spain.58.d1
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				spain_leninist_support > 2
			}
			check_variable = {
				spain_neocom_support < 3
			}
			check_variable = {
				spain_syndicalist_support < 3
			}
		}
	}
	desc = { #neocom victory
		text = spain.58.d2
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				spain_leninist_support < 3
			}
			check_variable = {
				spain_neocom_support > 2
			}
			check_variable = {
				spain_syndicalist_support < 3
			}
		}
	}
	desc = { #syndicalist
		text = spain.58.d3
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				spain_leninist_support < 3
			}
			check_variable = {
				spain_neocom_support < 3
			}
			check_variable = {
				spain_syndicalist_support > 2
			}
		}
	}
	desc = { #stalinist
		text = spain.58.d4
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				spain_leninist_support < 3
			}
			check_variable = {
				spain_neocom_support < 3
			}
			check_variable = {
				spain_syndicalist_support < 3
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #leninist victory
		name = spain.58.o1
		set_country_flag = spain_leninist_victory
		clr_country_flag = united_left_ministers
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
		IF = {
			limit = {tag = SPR}
			create_country_leader = {
				 name = "Enrique Santiago"
				 picture = Portrait_SPR_Enrique_Santiago.dds
				 ideology = leninist
			}
		}
		ELSE_IF = {
			limit = {tag = SPN}
			create_country_leader = {
				 name = "Enrique Santiago"
				 picture = Portrait_SPN_Enrique_Santiago.dds
				 ideology = leninist
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = SPR_thirdrep
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							tag = SPR
							tag = SPN
						}
					}
				}
				news_event = {
					id = spain_news.19
				}
			}
		}
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = communist
			elections_allowed = no
			last_election = "1935.12.17"
			election_frequency = 48
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_ideas = spr_sic_angeles_maestro
			add_ideas = spr_fom_sira_rego
			add_ideas = spr_ind_txema_guijarro
			add_ideas = spr_nsm_carmelo_antonio_suarez_cabrera
			add_ideas = spr_inm_willy_enrique_meyer_pleite
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = spain_leninist_ministers_tooltip
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = communist
			popularity = 0.15
		}
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				spain_leninist_support > 2
			}
			check_variable = {
				spain_neocom_support < 3
			}
			check_variable = {
				spain_syndicalist_support < 3
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #neocom victory
		name = spain.58.o2
		set_country_flag = spain_neocom_victory
		clr_country_flag = united_left_ministers
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = communist
				elections_allowed = no
				last_election = "1935.12.17"
				election_frequency = 48
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				add_ideas = spr_sic_gaspar_llamazares
				add_ideas = spr_fom_roser_maestro
				add_ideas = spr_ind_alberto_garzon
				add_ideas = spr_nsm_felipe_alcaraz
				add_ideas = spr_inm_cayo_lara
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							OR = {
								tag = SPR
								tag = SPN
							}
						}
					}
					news_event = {
						id = spain_news.20
					}
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = spain_neocom_ministers_tooltip
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = communist
				popularity = 0.15
			}
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				spain_leninist_support < 3
			}
			check_variable = {
				spain_neocom_support > 2
			}
			check_variable = {
				spain_syndicalist_support < 3
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #syndicalist victory
		name = spain.58.o3
		set_country_flag = spain_syndicalist_victory
		clr_country_flag = united_left_ministers
		mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = revolutionary_socialist
				long_name = SPR_UGT_long
				name = SPR_UGT
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				add_ideas = spr_sic_cristina_antonanzas
				add_ideas = spr_fom_cristinia_estevez
				add_ideas = spr_ind_jesus_gualix
				add_ideas = spr_nsm_luz_martinez_ten
				add_ideas = spr_inm_desiree_gallardo
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							OR = {
								tag = SPR
								tag = SPN
							}
						}
					}
					news_event = {
						id = spain_news.21
					}
				}
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = spain_syndie_ministers_tooltip
			IF = {
				limit = {tag = SPR}
				create_country_leader = {
					 name = "Pepe Álvarez"
					 picture = Portrait_SPR_Jose_Maria_Alvarez_Suarez.dds
					 ideology = syndicalism
				}
			}
			ELSE_IF = {
				limit = {tag = SPN}
				create_country_leader = {
					 name = "Pepe Álvarez"
					 picture = Portrait_SPN_Jose_Maria_Alvarez_Suarez.dds
					 ideology = syndicalism
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				set_cosmetic_tag = SPR_thirdrep
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = revolutionary_socialist
				popularity = 0.15
			}
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				spain_leninist_support < 3
			}
			check_variable = {
				spain_neocom_support < 3
			}
			check_variable = {
				spain_syndicalist_support > 2
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #stalinist
		name = spain.58.o4
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = spain_stalinist_victory

								}
							}
							set_technology = {
								armored_car1 = 1
							}
						}
					}
					931 = {
						create_unit = {
							division = "name = \"Community Defense Militia\" division_template = \"Community Defense Militia\" start_experience_factor = 0.1 start_equipment_factor = 1"
							owner = CCM
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				tag = SPR
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_puppet_of = ROOT
				}
				add_ideas = {
					idea_spr_confederal_member_spr
				}
			}
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				tag = SPN
			}
			every_country = {
				limit = {
					is_puppet_of = ROOT
				}
				add_ideas = {
					idea_spr_confederal_member_spn
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#EQG declares independence after mobilizing guard
country_event = {
	id = spain.89
	title = spain.89.t
	desc = spain.89.d
	picture = spr_equatoguinean_rebels_declare_independence

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			tag = SPN
			tag = SPR
		}
		owns_state = 297
		OR = {
			has_war_with = SPR
			has_war_with = SPN
		}
		has_country_flag = spr_mobilized_eqg_guard
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 90
	}

	option = {
		name = spain.89.o1
		EQG = {
			transfer_state = 297
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = spain.89.o2
		EQG = {
			transfer_state = 297
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				tag = SPR
			}
			SPR = {
					declare_war_on = {
						type = annex_everything
						target = EQG
					}
			}
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				tag = SPN
			}
			SPN = {
					declare_war_on = {
						type = annex_everything
						target = EQG
					}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = spain.89.o3
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
		EQG = {
			transfer_state = 297
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				tag = SPR
			}
			EQG = {
				change_tag_from = SPR
			}
			SPR = {
					declare_war_on = {
						type = annex_everything
						target = EQG
					}
			}
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				tag = SPN
			}
			EQG = {
				change_tag_from = SPN
			}
			SPN = {
					declare_war_on = {
						type = annex_everything
						target = EQG
					}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Javier I sworn in as King of the Spaniards
country_event = {
	id = spain.145
	title = spain.145.t
	desc = spain.145.d
	picture = spr_carlos_javier_denounces_republicanism

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = spain.145.o1
		IF = {
			limit = {
				tag = SPR
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				 name = "Carlos Javier I"
				 picture = Portrait_SPR_Carlos_Javier_I.dds
				 ideology = carlist_monarchist
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = monarchist
				long_name = spain_carlist_long
				name = spain_carlist
			}
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				tag = SPN
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				 name = "Carlos Javier I"
				 picture = Portrait_SPN_Carlos_Javier_I.dds
				 ideology = carlist_monarchist
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = monarchist
				long_name = spain_carlist_long
				name = spain_carlist
			}
		}
		add_ideas = {
			idea_spr_carlos_javier_i
		}
		add_ideas = {
			spr_sic_carlos_javier_I
		}
		set_cosmetic_tag = SPR_cons_carlist
		complete_national_focus = SPR_newdem_election_victory
		set_politics = {
			ruling_party = new_democrat
			elections_allowed = no
			last_election = "1935.12.17"
			election_frequency = 48
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_ideas = spr_fom_jose_manuel_albares
			add_ideas = spr_ind_elena_salgado
			add_ideas = spr_nsm_margarita_robles
			add_ideas = spr_inm_alfredo_perez_rubalcaba
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							OR = {
								tag = SPR
								tag = SPN
							}
						}
					}
					news_event = {
						id = spain_news.33
					}
				}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = spain_newdem_ministers_tooltip
		add_popularity = {
			ideology = new_democrat
			popularity = 0.15
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = idea_SPR_limited_suffrage
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = idea_SPR_limited_suffrage
				add_idea = idea_SPR_universal_suffrage_2
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = constitutional_carlism
	}
}

#Equatorial Guinea demands independence referendum after right coalition
country_event = {
	id = spain.156
	title = spain.156.t
	desc = spain.156.d
	picture = spr_eqg_votes_for_independence

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			tag = SPR
			tag = SPN
		}
		owns_state = 297
		OR = {
			has_completed_focus = SPR_limited_suffrage
			has_completed_focus = SPR_universal_suffrage
			has_completed_focus = SPR_a_confederate_spain
			has_completed_focus = SPR_a_federal_spain
			has_completed_focus = SPR_codify_regional_autonomy
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 14
	}

	option = { #let us guide them to democracy
		name = spain.156.o1
		ai_chance = {base = 25}
		release = EQG
		EQG = {
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = centrist
				elections_allowed = no
				last_election = "1935.12.17"
				election_frequency = 48
			}
			give_resource_rights = {
				receiver = ROOT
				state = 297
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #EQG is spain!
		name = spain.156.o2
		ai_chance = {base = 75}
		297 = {
			add_resistance = 15
			add_compliance = -25
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = spain.157
				days = 30
			}
		}
	}
}

					 ideology = titoist
				}
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = revolutionary_socialist
				popularity = 0.15
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = monarchist
				elections_allowed = no
				last_election = "1935.12.17"
				election_frequency = 48
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = revolutionary_socialist
				long_name = spain_new_carlist_long
				name = spain_new_carlist
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = SPR_SFKS
		}
	}
}

		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = SPR_fopo_reclaim_eqg
			has_completed_focus = stalinist_recognize_citizenship_of_colonial_subjects
			has_completed_focus = SPR_titoist_fopo_reclaim_eqg
		}

		OR = {
			tag = SPR
			tag = SPN
		}
		has_war_with = EQG
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = SPR
		}
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = SPN
		}
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = CAT
		}
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = BSQ
		}
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = GAL
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 180
	}

	option = { #yes
		name = spain.168.o1
		ai_chance = {base = 100}
		white_peace = EQG
	}
	option = {
		name = spain.168.o2
		ai_chance = {base = 0}
	}
}
#basques rise up during the civil war
country_event = {
	id = spain.169
	title = spain.169.t
	desc = spain.169.d
	picture = spr_basque_country_revolts

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			tag = SPR
			tag = SPN
		}
		OR = {
			has_war_with = SPR
			has_war_with = SPN
		}
		OR = {
			has_government = fascist
			has_government = monarchist
		}
		OR = {
			controls_state = 1020
			AND = {
				controls_state = 1020
				owns_state = 1020
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			1020 = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = autonomous_state }
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			country_exists = BSQ
		}
		NOT = {
			has_country_flag = SPR_the_basques_rebelled
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 150
	}
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {    #stay with spain
		name = spain.169.o1
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = BSQ
				}
				remove_core_of = SPN
				remove_core_of = SPR
			}
			IF = {
				limit = {
					tag = SPR
				}
				SPR = {
					retire_character = SPR_Antonio_Martorell_Lacave
					retire_character = SPR_Carlos_Villar_Turrau
				}
			}
			IF = {
				limit = {
					tag = SPN
				}
				SPN = {
					retire_character = SPN_Antonio_Martorell_Lacave
					retire_character = SPN_Carlos_Villar_Turrau
				}
			}
		}
		BSQ = {
			transfer_state = 1020
			transfer_state = 172
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			BSQ = {load_oob = BSQ_Revolution}
			SPR = {
				BSQ = {
					transfer_technology = yes
				}
			}
			SPR = {
				IF = {
					limit = {has_country_flag = BSQ_real_mad}
					BSQ = {load_oob = BSQ_Extra}
				}
			}
			BSQ = {
				add_naval_commander_role = {
					Character = BSQ_Antonio_Martorell_Lacave
					traits={ fly_swatter }
					skill=2
					attack_skill=2
					defense_skill=2
					maneuvering_skill=1
					coordination_skill=3
				}
				add_advisor_role = {
					character = BSQ_Antonio_Martorell_Lacave
					advisor = {
						slot = navy_chief
						idea_token = BSQ_Antonio_Martorell_Lacave
						traits = {
							navy_chief_decisive_battle_2 
						}
					}
				}
				add_corps_commander_role = {
					Character = BSQ_Carlos_Villar_Turrau
					traits={ infantry_officer infantry_leader trait_cautious }
					skill=2
					attack_skill=2
					defense_skill=2
					planning_skill=3
					logistics_skill=1
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = train_equipment
					amount = 50
				}
			}
		}
		ROOT = {
			declare_war_on = { target = BSQ type = annex_everything }
		}
	}
	option = {    #basques
		name = spain.169.o2
		hidden_effect = {
			BSQ = {load_oob = BSQ_Revolution}
			SPR = {
				BSQ = {
					transfer_technology = yes
				}
			}
			SPR = {
				IF = {
					limit = {has_country_flag = BSQ_real_mad}
					BSQ = {load_oob = BSQ_Extra}
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = BSQ
				}
				remove_core_of = SPR
				remove_core_of = SPN
			}
			IF = {
				limit = {
					tag = SPR
				}
				SPR = {
					retire_character = SPR_Antonio_Martorell_Lacave
					retire_character = SPR_Carlos_Villar_Turrau
				}
			}
			IF = {
				limit = {
					tag = SPN
				}
				SPN = {
					retire_character = SPN_Antonio_Martorell_Lacave
					retire_character = SPN_Carlos_Villar_Turrau
				}
			}
			BSQ = {
				add_naval_commander_role = {
					Character = BSQ_Antonio_Martorell_Lacave
					traits={ fly_swatter }
					skill=2
					attack_skill=2
					defense_skill=2
					maneuvering_skill=1
					coordination_skill=3
				}
				add_advisor_role = {
					character = BSQ_Antonio_Martorell_Lacave
					advisor = {
						slot = navy_chief
						idea_token = BSQ_Antonio_Martorell_Lacave
						traits = {
							navy_chief_decisive_battle_2 
						}
					}
				}
				add_corps_commander_role = {
					Character = BSQ_Carlos_Villar_Turrau
					traits={ infantry_officer infantry_leader trait_cautious }
					skill=2
					attack_skill=2
					defense_skill=2
					planning_skill=3
					logistics_skill=1
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = train_equipment
					amount = 50
				}
			}
		}
		BSQ = {
			transfer_state = 1020
			transfer_state = 172
		}
		ROOT = {
			declare_war_on = { target = BSQ type = annex_everything }
		}
		BSQ = {
            change_tag_from = ROOT
        }
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = spain.170
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			base = 0
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = spain.171
	title = spain.171.t
	desc = spain.171.d
	picture = spr_galicia_revolts

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			tag = SPR
			tag = SPN
		}
		OR = {
			has_war_with = SPR
			has_war_with = SPN
		}
		OR = {
			has_government = fascist
			has_government = monarchist
		}
		OR = {
			controls_state = 171
			AND = {
				controls_state = 171
				owns_state = 171
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			171 = {
				has_dynamic_modifier = { modifier = autonomous_state }
			}
		}
		NOT = {
			country_exists = GAL
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 300
	}
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {    #stay with spain
		name = spain.171.o1
		hidden_effect = {
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = GAL
				}
				remove_core_of = SPN
				remove_core_of = SPR
			}
		}
		GAL = {
			transfer_state = 171
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			GAL = {load_oob = GAL_Revolution}
			SPR = {
				GAL = {
					transfer_technology = yes
				}
			}
			SPR = {
				IF = {
					limit = {has_country_flag = GAL_real_mad}
					GAL = {load_oob = GAL_Extra}
				}
			}
			SPR = {
				retire_character = SPR_Fernando_Lens_Astray
				retire_character = SPR_Jose_Julio_Rodriguez_Fernandez
			}
			GAL = {
				add_corps_commander_role = {
					Character = GAL_Jose_Julio_Rodriguez_Fernandez
					traits={ commando inflexible_strategist trait_reckless }
					skill=2
					attack_skill=2
					defense_skill=2
					planning_skill=1
					logistics_skill=2
				}
				add_corps_commander_role = {
					Character = GAL_Fernando_Lens_Astray
					traits={ armor_officer harsh_leader trait_reckless }
					skill=3
					attack_skill=3
					defense_skill=2
					planning_skill=2
					logistics_skill=1
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = train_equipment
					amount = 50
				}
			}
		}
		ROOT = {
			declare_war_on = { target = GAL type = annex_everything }
		}
	}
	option = {    #galicians
		name = spain.171.o2
		hidden_effect = {
			GAL = {load_oob = GAL_Revolution}
			SPR = {
				GAL = {
					transfer_technology = yes
				}
			}
			SPR = {
				IF = {
					limit = {has_country_flag = GAL_real_mad}
					GAL = {load_oob = GAL_Extra}
				}
			}
			every_state = {
				limit = {
					is_core_of = GAL
				}
				remove_core_of = SPR
				remove_core_of = SPN
			}
			SPR = {
				retire_character = SPR_Fernando_Lens_Astray
				retire_character = SPR_Jose_Julio_Rodriguez_Fernandez
			}
			GAL = {
				add_corps_commander_role = {
					Character = GAL_Jose_Julio_Rodriguez_Fernandez
					traits={ commando inflexible_strategist trait_reckless }
					skill=2
					attack_skill=2
					defense_skill=2
					planning_skill=1
					logistics_skill=2
				}
				add_corps_commander_role = {

#tejero wants to enlist
country_event = {
	id = spain.236
	title = spain.236.t
	desc = spain.236.d
	picture = spr_tejero_time
	trigger = {
		OR = {
			tag = SPR
			tag = SPN
		}
		OR = {
			has_war_with = SPR
			has_war_with = SPN
		}
		has_government = fascist
	}
	fire_only_once = yes
	option = {
		name = spain.236.o1
		ai_chance = {
			base = 99
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				tag = SPR
			}
			add_corps_commander_role = {
				Character = SPR_Antonio_Tejero
				traits={ old_guard politically_connected war_hero career_officer trait_reckless media_personality harsh_leader }
				skill=4
				attack_skill=4
				defense_skill=3
				planning_skill=1
				logistics_skill=3
			}
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				tag = SPN
			}
			add_corps_commander_role = {
				Character = SPN_Antonio_Tejero
				traits={ old_guard politically_connected war_hero career_officer trait_reckless media_personality harsh_leader }
				skill=4
				attack_skill=4
				defense_skill=3
				planning_skill=1
				logistics_skill=3
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = spr_recruited_tejero
		add_stability = -0.01
	}
	option = {
		name = spain.236.o2
		ai_chance = {
			base = 1
		}
		set_country_flag = spr_denied_tejero
	}
}

#a united workers front
country_event = {
	id = spain.340
	title = spain.340.t
	desc = spain.340.d
	picture = spr_stalin_unification

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = spain.340.o1
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = communist
			long_name = "Communist Party of Spain - Hardliners"
			name = "Communist Party - H"
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = revolutionary_socialist
			long_name = "Communist Party of Spain - Syndicalists"
			name = "Communist Party - S"
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = moderate_socialist
			long_name = "Communist Party of Spain - Reformists"
			name = "Communist Party - R"
		}
		set_party_name = {
			ideology = new_democrat
			long_name = "Communist Party of Spain - Liberals"
			name = "Communist Party - L"
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			IF = {
				limit = { tag = SPR }
				create_country_leader = {
					 name = "Workers' Commissions"
					 picture = Portrait__SPR_CCOO.dds
					 ideology = orthodox_leninist
				}
			}
			IF = {
				limit = { tag = SPN }
				create_country_leader = {
					 name = "Workers' Commissions"
					 picture = Portrait__SPN_CCOO.dds
					 ideology = orthodox_leninist
				}
			}
			IF = {
				limit = { tag = SPR }
				create_country_leader = {
					 name = "Yolanda Diaz"
					 picture = Portrait_SPR_Yolanda_Diaz.dds
					 ideology = peoples_socialist_democracy
				}
			}
			IF = {
				limit = { tag = SPN }
				create_country_leader = {
					 name = "Yolanda Diaz"
					 picture = Portrait_SPN_Yolanda_Diaz.dds
					 ideology = peoples_socialist_democracy
				}
			}
			IF = {
				limit = { tag = SPR }
				create_country_leader = {
					 name = "José María González Santos"
					 picture = Portrait_SPR_Jose_Maria_Gonzalez_Santos.dds
					 ideology = labourist
				}
			}
			IF = {
				limit = { tag = SPN }
				create_country_leader = {
					 name = "José María González Santos"
					 picture = Portrait_SPN_Jose_Maria_Gonzalez_Santos.dds
					 ideology = labourist
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#eta asks for amnesty
country_event = {
	id = spain.388
	title = spain.388.t
	desc = spain.388.d
	picture = spr_eta_wants_amnesty

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #forgive and forget
		name = spain.388.o1
		set_country_flag = spr_forgave_eta
		add_stability = -0.03
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = BSQ
				NOT = {
					is_core_of = ROOT
				}
			}
			add_compliance = 10
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = spain.389
				days = 7
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #no, imprison them
		name = spain.388.o2
		set_country_flag = spr_didnt_forgive_eta
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = spain.389
				days = 7
			}
		}
	}
}

#get rid of SPR cores
country_event = {
	id = spain.800
	title = spain.800.t
	desc = spain.800.d
	picture = GFX_carlos_sick
	hidden = yes


	trigger = {
		tag = SPN
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = SPR
		}
		has_country_flag = spanish_civil_war
	}

	fire_only_once = yes
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 90
	}

	option = {
		name = spain.800.a
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = SPN
			}
			remove_core_of = SPR
		}
	}
}

#Nationalist Spain is fucked, they must surrender
country_event = {
	id = spain.803
	title = spain.803.t
	desc = spain.803.d
	picture = spr_humiliating_defeat

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			tag = SPR
			tag = SPN
		}
		has_country_flag = catalan_war
		has_war_with = CAT
		surrender_progress > 0.75
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = SPN
		}
		NOT = {
			has_war_with = SPR
		}
		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = SPR_republican_coup
		}
		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = SPR_military_coup
		}
		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = SPR_felipe_stays
		}
		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = carlist_el_rey_rojo
		}
		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = stalinist_factional_deadlock
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}

	option = { #sign peace
		name = spain.803.a
		CAT = {
			transfer_state = 167
			transfer_state = 177
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			white_peace = GAL
			white_peace = BSQ
			white_peace = CAT
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {country_exists = SPN}
			SPN = {
				annex_country = {
					target = SPR
					transfer_troops = no
				}
			}
		}
		ELSE = {
			remove_ideas = {idea_SPR_subversives_organizing}
			set_country_flag = military_coup
			mark_focus_tree_layout_dirty = yes
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = fascist
				long_name = SPR_Military_Administration_long
				name = SPR_Military_Administration
			}
			create_country_leader = {
				 name = "Fulgencio Coll Bucher"
				 picture = Portrait_SPR_Fulgencio_Coll_Bucher.dds
				 ideology = francoist
			}
			set_politics = {
				ruling_party = fascist
				elections_allowed = no
				last_election = "1935.12.17"
				election_frequency = 48
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = nationalist
				popularity = 0.06
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = fascist
				popularity = 0.20
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = national_bolshevik
				popularity = 0.15
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = monarchist
				popularity = -0.10
			}
			set_variable = {military_anger = 0}
		}
	}
}
#Republican Spain can fight the secessionists
country_event = {
	id = spain.804
	title = spain.804.t
	desc = spain.804.d
	picture = spr_matter_of_secessionists

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #maintain peace with the secessionists
		name = spain.804.a
		ai_chance = { base = 95 }

	}
	option = { #fight the secessionists
		name = spain.804.b
		ai_chance = { base = 5 }
		set_country_flag = catalan_war
		SPN = {
			IF = {
				limit = {country_exists = CAT}
				declare_war_on = { target = CAT type = annex_everything }
			}
			IF = {
				limit = {country_exists = BSQ}
				declare_war_on = { target = BSQ type = annex_everything }
			}
			IF = {
				limit = {country_exists = GAL}
				declare_war_on = { target = GAL type = annex_everything }
			}
		}
	}
}
#Spanish battle royale has gone sideways, spain must surrender
country_event = {
	id = spain.805
	title = spain.805.t
	desc = spain.805.d
	picture = spr_humiliating_defeat

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			tag = SPR
			tag = SPN
		}
		OR = {
			has_war_with = SPR
			has_war_with = SPN
		}
		OR = {
			has_war_with = GAL
			has_war_with = BSQ
			has_war_with = CAT
		}
		surrender_progress > 0.75
		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = SPR_republican_coup
		}
		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = SPR_military_coup
		}
		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = SPR_felipe_stays
		}
		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = carlist_el_rey_rojo
		}
		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = stalinist_factional_deadlock
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}

	option = { #sign peace
		name = spain.805.a
		IF = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = CAT
			}
			CAT = {
				transfer_state = 167
				transfer_state = 177
				transfer_state = 911
				transfer_state = 852
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			white_peace = GAL
			white_peace = BSQ
			white_peace = CAT
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				tag = SPR
				has_war_with = SPN
			}
			SPN = {
				annex_country = {
					target = SPR
					transfer_troops = no
				}
			}
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				tag = SPN
				has_war_with = SPR
			}
			SPR = {
				annex_country = {
					target = SPN
					transfer_troops = no
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Carlist Titoists reach out to Yugoslavia
country_event = {
	id = spain_diplo.1
	title = spain_diplo.1.t
	desc = spain_diplo.1.d
	picture = spr_dip_yugo

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #happy to trade
		name = spain_diplo.1.o1
		ai_chance = {base = 95}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					country_exists = SPR
					SPR = {
						has_government = revolutionary_socialist
					}
				}
			}
			SPR = {
				country_event = {
					id = spain_diplo.2
				}
			}
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					country_exists = SPN
					SPN = {
						has_government = revolutionary_socialist
					}
				}
			}
			SPN = {
				country_event = {
					id = spain_diplo.2
				}
			}
		}
		add_resource = {
			type = steel
			amount = 15
			state = 107
		}
		107 = {
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_building_construction = {
				type = infrastructure
				level = 1
				instant_build = yes
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #fuck off
		name = spain_diplo.1.o2
		ai_chance = {base = 5}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					country_exists = SPR
					SPR = {
						has_government = revolutionary_socialist
					}
				}
			}
			SPR = {
				country_event = {
					id = spain_diplo.3
				}
			}
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				AND = {
					country_exists = SPN
					SPN = {
						has_government = revolutionary_socialist
					}
				}
			}
			SPN = {
				country_event = {
					id = spain_diplo.3
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	option = { #happy to trade

#Catalonia accepts
country_event = {
	id = spain_diplo.20
	title = spain_diplo.20.t
	desc = spain_diplo.20.d
	picture = spr_dip_breakaway_yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #yay!
		name = spain_diplo.20.o1
		IF = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = SPR_a_confederate_spain
				NOT = {
					has_completed_focus = SPR_nat_reunite_spain
				}
				NOT = {
					has_completed_focus = SPR_liberal_recentralize_spain
				}
			}
			puppet = CAT
			CAT = {
				set_cosmetic_tag = CAT_autonomous
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				CAT = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = new_democrat
						elections_allowed = no
						last_election = "1935.12.17"
						election_frequency = 48
					}
					load_focus_tree = generic_focus
				}
			}
		}
		ELSE_IF = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					NOT = {
						has_completed_focus = SPR_a_confederate_spain
					}
					has_completed_focus = SPR_nat_reunite_spain
					has_completed_focus = SPR_liberal_recentralize_spain
				}
			}
			annex_country = {
				target = CAT
				transfer_troops = yes
			}
		}
	}
}
#Catalonia declines

		name = spain_diplo.29.o1
		set_country_flag = spr_country_agreed_to_non_aggression
		ai_chance = {base = 70}

			limit = {
				country_exists = SPR
			}

				country_event = {
					id = spain_diplo.30
				}
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = ROOT
					relation = non_aggression_pact
					active = yes
				}
			}
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = SPN
			}
			SPN = {
				country_event = {
					id = spain_diplo.30
				}
				diplomatic_relation = {
					country = ROOT
					relation = non_aggression_pact
					active = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #fuck off
		name = spain_diplo.29.o2
		ai_chance = {
			base = 30
			modifier = {
				factor = 0
				FROM = {
					has_government = ROOT
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = spr_country_refused_non_aggression
		IF = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = SPR
			}
			SPR = {
				country_event = {
					id = spain_diplo.31
				}
			}
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = SPN
			}
			SPN = {
				country_event = {
					id = spain_diplo.31
				}
			}
		}
	}

#Portugal accepts
country_event = {
	id = spain_diplo.57
	title = spain_diplo.57.t
	desc = spain_diplo.57.d
	picture = spr_spain_portugal_unify_yes

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #yay!
		name = spain_diplo.57.o1
		annex_country = {
			target = POR
			transfer_troops = yes
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = POR
			}
			add_core_of = ROOT
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_completed_focus = carlist_el_rey_rojo
				}
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = spr_picked_wreath_over_crown
				}
				NOT = {
					has_government = communist
				}
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = SPR_republican_iberia
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_completed_focus = carlist_el_rey_rojo
				}
				has_country_flag = spr_picked_wreath_over_crown
				NOT = {
					has_government = communist
				}
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = SPR_republican_iberia_wreath
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				has_government = revolutionary_socialist
				has_completed_focus = carlist_el_rey_rojo
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = SPR_titoist_kingdom_of_iberia
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_completed_focus = SPR_leninist_victory
				}
				has_government = communist
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = SPR_fprs
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				has_completed_focus = SPR_leninist_victory
				has_government = communist
			}
			set_cosmetic_tag = SPR_fprs_lenin
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = communist
				long_name = "Communist Party of Iberia"
				name = "Communist Party"
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = centrist
				long_name = "One Iberia"
				name = "One Iberia"
			}
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = new_democrat
				long_name = "Iberian Socialist Workers' Party"
				name = "Socialist Party"
			}
		}
	}
}

#Iberian Mutual Defense Pact ratified
country_event = {
	id = spain_diplo.77
	title = spain_diplo.77.t

	desc = { #no one signs
		text = spain_diplo.77.d1
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				check_variable = {
					iberian_defense_pact_signatories = 0
				}

			}
		}
	}
	desc = { #a few sign
		text = spain_diplo.77.d2
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					check_variable = {
						iberian_defense_pact_signatories = 1
					}
					check_variable = {
						valid_independent_spanish_states > 1
					}
				}
				AND = {
					check_variable = {
						iberian_defense_pact_signatories = 2
					}
					check_variable = {
						valid_independent_spanish_states > 2
					}
				}		
				AND = {
					check_variable = {
						iberian_defense_pact_signatories = 3
					}
					check_variable = {
						valid_independent_spanish_states > 3
					}
				}			
				AND = {
					check_variable = {
						iberian_defense_pact_signatories = 4
					}
					check_variable = {
						valid_independent_spanish_states > 4
					}
				}	
				AND = {
					check_variable = {
						iberian_defense_pact_signatories = 5
					}
					check_variable = {
						valid_independent_spanish_states > 5
					}
				}	
			}
		}
	}
	desc = { #everyone signed
		text = spain_diplo.77.d3
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					check_variable = {
						iberian_defense_pact_signatories = 1
					}
					check_variable = {
						valid_independent_spanish_states = 1
					}
				}
				AND = {
					check_variable = {
						iberian_defense_pact_signatories = 2
					}
					check_variable = {
						valid_independent_spanish_states = 2
					}
				}
				AND = {
					check_variable = {
						iberian_defense_pact_signatories = 3
					}
					check_variable = {
						valid_independent_spanish_states = 3
					}
				}
				AND = {
					check_variable = {
						iberian_defense_pact_signatories = 4
					}
					check_variable = {
						valid_independent_spanish_states = 4
					}
				}
				AND = {
					check_variable = {
						iberian_defense_pact_signatories = 5
					}
					check_variable = {
						valid_independent_spanish_states = 5
					}
				}
				AND = {
					check_variable = {
						iberian_defense_pact_signatories = 6
					}
					check_variable = {
						valid_independent_spanish_states = 6
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	picture = spr_iberian_defense_final

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 1
	}

	option = { #everyone signed
		name = spain_diplo.77.o1
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				BSQ = {
					has_country_flag = spr_iberian_defense_pact_signatory
				}
				CAT = {
					has_country_flag = spr_iberian_defense_pact_signatory
				}
				GAL = {
					has_country_flag = spr_iberian_defense_pact_signatory
				}
			}
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				BSQ = {
					has_country_flag = spr_iberian_defense_pact_signatory
				}
			}
			BSQ = {
				give_guarantee = ROOT
			}
			give_guarantee = BSQ
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				CAT = {
					has_country_flag = spr_iberian_defense_pact_signatory
				}
			}
			CAT = {
				give_guarantee = ROOT
			}
			give_guarantee = CAT
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				GAL = {

			}
			BSQ = {
				give_guarantee = GAL
			}
			GAL = {
				give_guarantee = BSQ
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #some signed
		name = spain_diplo.77.o2
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				check_variable = {
					iberian_defense_pact_signatories < 3
				}
				check_variable = {
					iberian_defense_pact_signatories > 0
				}
			}
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				BSQ = {
					has_country_flag = spr_iberian_defense_pact_signatory
				}
			}
			BSQ = {
				give_guarantee = ROOT
			}
			give_guarantee = BSQ
		}
		IF = {

				}
			}
			CAT = {
				give_guarantee = ROOT
			}
			give_guarantee = CAT
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				GAL = {
					has_country_flag = spr_iberian_defense_pact_signatory
				}
			}
			GAL = {
				give_guarantee = ROOT
			}
			give_guarantee = GAL
		}
		IF = {

					}
					CAT = {
						has_country_flag = spr_iberian_defense_pact_signatory
					}
				}
			}
			GAL = {
				give_guarantee = CAT
			}
			CAT = {
				give_guarantee = GAL
			}
		}

						has_country_flag = spr_iberian_defense_pact_signatory
					}
					CAT = {

					}
				}
			}
			BSQ = {
				give_guarantee = CAT

			}

		trigger = {

	desc = spain_diplo.128.d

	option = {
		name = spain_diplo.128.o1
		release_puppet = ANA
		IF = {
			limit = {
				tag = SPR
			}
			ANA = {
				add_ideas = {
					idea_spr_andorran_condominium_SPR
				}
			}
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				tag = SPN
			}
			ANA = {
				add_ideas = {
					idea_spr_andorran_condominium_SPN
				}
			}
		}
		diplomatic_relation = {
			country = FRA
			relation = non_aggression_pact
			active = yes
		}
		FRA = {
			diplomatic_relation = {
				country = ROOT
				relation = non_aggression_pact
				active = yes
			}
		}
		add_stability = 0.05
	}
}

#england is losing to Spain
country_event = {
	id = spain_diplo.139
	title = spain_diplo.139.t
	desc = spain_diplo.139.d
	picture = spr_gibraltar_stalemate

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = ENG
		OR = {
			AND = {
				country_exists = SPR
				has_war_with = SPR
				SPR = {
					OR = {
						has_completed_focus = SPR_fopo_the_gibraltar_issue
						has_completed_focus = SPR_stalinist_fopo_the_gibraltar_issue
						has_completed_focus = SPR_titoist_fopo_the_gibraltar_issue
					}
				}
				SPR = {
					surrender_progress < 0.15
					controls_state = 118
					is_in_faction = no
				}
			}
			AND = {
				country_exists = SPN
				has_war_with = SPN
				SPN = {
					OR = {
						has_completed_focus = SPR_fopo_the_gibraltar_issue
						has_completed_focus = SPR_stalinist_fopo_the_gibraltar_issue
						has_completed_focus = SPR_titoist_fopo_the_gibraltar_issue
					}
				}
				SPN = {
					surrender_progress < 0.10
					is_in_faction = no
					controls_state = 118
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 60
	}

	option = { #yes
		name = spain_diplo.139.o1
		ai_chance = {base = 100}

		IF = {
			limit = {
				country_exists = SPR
			}
			SPR = {
				country_event = {
					id = spain_diplo.140
					days = 3
				}
			}
		}
		IF = { 
			limit = {
				country_exists = SPN
			}
			SPN = {
				country_event = {
					id = spain_diplo.140
					days = 3
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #no
		name = spain_diplo.139.o2
		ai_chance = {base = 0}
		add_war_support = -0.05
	}
}

#morocco accepts
country_event = {
	id = spain_diplo.184
	title = spain_diplo.184.t
	desc = spain_diplo.184.d
	picture = spr_sahrawi_independence_yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = spain_diplo.184.o1
		puppet = WSA
		hidden_effect = {
			IF = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_government = fascist
						has_government = nationalist
					}
				}
				WSA = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = nationalist
						elections_allowed = no
						last_election = "1935.12.17"
						election_frequency = 48
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = nationalist
						popularity = 0.5
					}
				}
			}
			IF = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_government = monarchist
						has_government = national_conservative
						has_government = centrist
					}
				}
				WSA = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = national_conservative
						elections_allowed = no
						last_election = "1935.12.17"
						election_frequency = 48
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = national_conservative
						popularity = 0.5
					}
				}
			}
			IF = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_government = liberal
						has_government = new_democrat
						has_government = moderate_socialist
					}
				}
				WSA = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = liberal
						elections_allowed = no
						last_election = "1935.12.17"
						election_frequency = 48
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = liberal
						popularity = 0.5
					}
				}
			}
			IF = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						has_government = communist
						has_government = revolutionary_socialist
					}
				}
				WSA = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = revolutionary_socialist
						elections_allowed = no
						last_election = "1935.12.17"
						election_frequency = 48
					}
					add_popularity = {
						ideology = revolutionary_socialist
						popularity = 0.5
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	picture = spr_west_sahara_question

	is_triggered_only = yes

		name = spain_diplo.186.o1
		ai_chance = {base = 50}
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = nationalist
			}
		}
		end_puppet = WSA
	}
	option = { #continue "guiding" them
		name = spain_diplo.186.o2
		ai_chance = {base = 50}
	}
	option = { #prepare for a referendum
		name = spain_diplo.186.o3
		ai_chance = {
			base = 50
			modifier = {
				AND = {
					has_cosmetic_tag = SPR_confederate
					OR = {
						has_government = new_democrat
						has_government = moderate_socialist
					}
				}
				add = 100
			}
		}
		country_event = {
			id = spain_diplo.187
		}
		WSA = {
			country_event = {
				id = spain_diplo.188
			}
		}
	}
}

#referendum results
country_event = {
	id = spain_diplo.192
	title = spain_diplo.192.t
	desc = spain_diplo.192.d
	picture = spr_west_sahara_question_vote

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #become independent
		name = spain_diplo.192.o1
		ai_chance = {
			base = 80
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = spr_spain_did_political_campaign
				add = -40
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = spr_spain_invested_in_the_region
				add = -40
			}
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				is_puppet_of = SPR
			}
			SPR = {
				country_event = {
					id = spain_diplo.193
				}
			}
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				is_puppet_of = SPN
			}
			SPN = {
				country_event = {
					id = spain_diplo.193
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #become part of Spain
		name = spain_diplo.192.o2
		ai_chance = {
			base = 20
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = spr_spain_did_political_campaign
				add = 40
			}
			modifier = {
				has_country_flag = spr_spain_invested_in_the_region
				add = 40
			}
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				is_puppet_of = SPR
			}
			SPR = {
				country_event = {
					id = spain_diplo.194
				}
			}
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				is_puppet_of = SPN
			}
			SPN = {
				country_event = {
					id = spain_diplo.194
				}
			}
		}
	}
}
#sahrawi decides to be independent
country_event = {
	id = spain_diplo.193
	title = spain_diplo.193.t
	desc = spain_diplo.193.d
	picture = spr_west_sahara_wants_independence

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #let them go
		name = spain_diplo.193.o1
		end_puppet = WSA
	}
	option = { #kill the sahrawis
		name = spain_diplo.193.o2
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_government = nationalist
				has_government = national_conservative
				has_government = monarchist
			}
		}
		end_puppet = WSA
		create_wargoal = {
			type = annex_everything
			target = WSA
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = WSA
			}
			add_claim_by = ROOT
		}
	}
}
#sahrawi agrees to integration
country_event = {
	id = spain_diplo.194
	title = spain_diplo.194.t
	desc = spain_diplo.194.d
	picture = spr_sahrawi_independence

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #they join spain
		name = spain_diplo.194.o1
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				has_cosmetic_tag = SPR_confederate
			}
		}
		annex_country = {
			target = WSA
			transfer_troops = yes
		}
		every_state = {
			limit = {
				is_core_of = WSA
			}
			add_core_of = ROOT
		}
	}
	option = { #they join spanish confederation
		name = spain_diplo.194.o2
		trigger = {
			has_cosmetic_tag = SPR_confederate
		}
		WSA = {
			set_cosmetic_tag = WSA_conf
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				tag = SPR
			}
			WSA = {
				add_ideas = {
					idea_spr_confederal_member_spr
				}
			}
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				tag = SPN
			}
			WSA = {
				add_ideas = {
					idea_spr_confederal_member_spn
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = spain_diplo.197
	title = spain_diplo.197.t
	desc = spain_diplo.197.d
	picture = spr_british_intervention

	trigger = {
		SPR = {
			has_war_with = SPN
		}
		tag = ENG
		ENG = {
			has_country_leader = {
				name = "Jeremy Corbyn"
				ruling_only = yes
			}
		}
	}
	fire_only_once = yes

	option = {
		name = spain_diplo.197.o1
		ai_chance = {base = 100}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				SPN = {
					has_government = moderate_socialist
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = corbyn_is_supporting_SPN
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = send_lend_lease_desire
				id = SPN
				value = 500
			}
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = send_volunteers_desire
				id = SPN
				value = 500
			}
			send_equipment = {
				equipment = infantry_equipment
				amount = 3000
				target = SPN
			}
			send_equipment = {
				equipment = artillery_equipment
				amount = 1000
				target = SPN
			}
			send_equipment = {
				equipment = support_equipment
				amount = 1000
				target = SPN
			}
			SPN = {
				country_event = {
					id = spain_diplo.198
				}
			}
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				SPR = {
					has_government = moderate_socialist
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = corbyn_is_supporting_SPR
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = send_lend_lease_desire
				id = SPR
				value = 500
			}
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = send_volunteers_desire
				id = SPR
				value = 500
			}
			send_equipment = {
				equipment = infantry_equipment
				amount = 3000
				target = SPR
			}
			send_equipment = {
				equipment = artillery_equipment
				amount = 1000
				target = SPR
			}
			send_equipment = {
				equipment = support_equipment
				amount = 1000
				target = SPR
			}
			SPR = {
				country_event = {
					id = spain_diplo.198
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = spain_diplo.197.o2
		ai_chance = {base = 0}
		
	}
}

						idea_cat_francoist_law_enforcement

			}
			IF = {
				limit = {
					tag = SPN
				}

						idea_spr_confederal_member_spn
					}
				}
			}
			IF = {
				limit = {
					tag = SPR
				}

				}

						monarchist = 0
						nationalist = 1
						centrist = 2
						fascist = 3
						liberal = 0
						communist = 2
					}
					remove_ideas = {
						idea_gal_divided_revolution
						idea_gal_legacy_resistance
					}
					load_focus_tree = generic_focus
				}
			}
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				owns_state = 1020
			}

				set_cosmetic_tag = BSQ_autonomous
			}
			IF = {
				limit = {

				}

						idea_spr_confederal_member_spn

				}

				retire_character = SPR_Carlos_Villar_Turrau
				BSQ = {
					set_politics = {
						ruling_party = new_democrat

	}

		name = spain_diplo.204.o2
		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				SPR = {
					OR = {
						has_government = monarchist
						has_government = fascist
					}
				}
			}
			send_equipment = {
				equipment = infantry_equipment
				amount = 3000
				target = SPR
			}
			send_equipment = {
				equipment = artillery_equipment
				amount = 100
				target = SPR
			}
			send_equipment = {
				equipment = support_equipment
				amount = 500
				target = SPR
			}
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				SPR = {
					OR = {
						has_government = monarchist
						has_government = fascist
					}
				}
			}
			send_equipment = {
				equipment = infantry_equipment
				amount = 3000
				target = SPR
			}
			send_equipment = {
				equipment = artillery_equipment
				amount = 100
				target = SPR
			}
			send_equipment = {
				equipment = support_equipment
				amount = 500
				target = SPR
			}
		}
		add_named_threat = {
			threat = 0.25
			name = spanish_intervention_threat
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			FROM = {
				country_event = {
					id = spain_diplo.207
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #send nothing

		ai_chance = {
			base = 25
		}
	}

#uk stops supporting spain
country_event = {
	id = spain_diplo.212
	title = spain_diplo.212.t
	desc = spain_diplo.212.d
	picture = x
	hidden = yes
	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = ENG
		OR = {
			NOT = {
				has_government = moderate_socialist
			}
			NOT = {
				SPN = {
					has_war_with = SPR
				}
			}
		}
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = corbyn_is_supporting_SPN
			has_country_flag = corbyn_is_supporting_SPR
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = spain_diplo.212.o1
		IF = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = corbyn_is_supporting_SPR
			}
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = send_lend_lease_desire
				id = SPR
				value = -500
			}
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = send_volunteers_desire
				id = SPR
				value = -500
			}
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = corbyn_is_supporting_SPN
			}
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = send_lend_lease_desire
				id = SPN
				value = -500
			}
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = send_volunteers_desire
				id = SPN
				value = -500
			}
		}
	}
}

#countries stop supporting spain
country_event = {
	id = spain_diplo.213
	title = spain_diplo.213.t
	desc = spain_diplo.213.d
	picture = x

	hidden = yes

	trigger = {
		OR = {
			has_country_flag = country_is_supporting_leftist_SPR_in_civil_war
			has_country_flag = country_is_supporting_leftist_SPN_in_civil_war
			has_country_flag = country_is_supporting_fascist_SPR_in_civil_war
			has_country_flag = country_is_supporting_fascist_SPN_in_civil_war
		}
		NOT = {
			SPR = {
				has_war_with = SPN
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = spain_diplo.212.o1
		IF = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = country_is_supporting_leftist_SPR_in_civil_war
					has_country_flag = country_is_supporting_fascist_SPR_in_civil_war
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = country_is_supporting_fascist_SPR_in_civil_war
			clr_country_flag = country_is_supporting_leftist_SPR_in_civil_war
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = send_lend_lease_desire
				id = SPR
				value = -500
			}
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = send_volunteers_desire
				id = SPR
				value = -500
			}
		}
		IF = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = country_is_supporting_leftist_SPN_in_civil_war
					has_country_flag = country_is_supporting_fascist_SPN_in_civil_war
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = country_is_supporting_fascist_SPN_in_civil_war
			clr_country_flag = country_is_supporting_leftist_SPN_in_civil_war
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = send_lend_lease_desire
				id = SPN
				value = -500
			}
			add_ai_strategy = {
				type = send_volunteers_desire
				id = SPN
				value = -500
			}
		}
	}
}

				tag = SPN

				 name = "Juan Carlos Monedero"

			}
		}
	}
}

			last_election = "1935.12.17"
			election_frequency = 48
		}

		}

					}
				}

			complete_national_focus = SPR_united_we_can

country_event = {
	id = spain_elections.9
	title = spain_elections.9.t
	desc = spain_elections.9.d
	picture = spr_santamaria

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = spain_elections.9.o1
		IF = {
			limit = { tag = SPR }
			create_country_leader = {
				 name = "Soraya Sáenz de Santamaría"
				 picture = Portrait_SPR_Soraya_Saenz_de_Santamaria.dds
				 ideology = christian_democrat
			}
		}
		IF = {
			limit = { tag = SPN }
			create_country_leader = {
				 name = "Soraya Sáenz de Santamaría"
				 picture = Portrait_SPN_Soraya_Saenz_de_Santamaria.dds
				 ideology = christian_democrat
			}
		}
	}
}

	desc = spain_elections.17.d
	picture = spr_gonzalez_santos

		name = spain_elections.17.o1
		IF = {
			limit = { tag = SPR }

				 name = "José María González Santos"

			}
		}

				 name = "José María González Santos"

			}
		}
	}

		}
	}
	desc = { #cannot newdems

		trigger = {

	}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #newdems win
		name = spain_elections.31.o2

			}
		}

		}

					}

		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = spain_newdem_ministers_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			IF = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_completed_focus = SPR_newdem_election_victory
					}
				}

		}

				limit = {
					NOT = {
						has_idea = spr_sic_felipe_vi
					}
				}
				add_ideas = spr_sic_tomas_marcos
			}
			add_ideas = spr_fom_arancha_gonzalez_laya
			add_ideas = spr_ind_toni_raldan
			add_ideas = spr_nsm_rosa_diez
			add_ideas = spr_inm_jorge_soler_gonzalez
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = spain_liberal_ministers_tooltip
		hidden_effect = {
			IF = {

				complete_national_focus = SPR_liberal_election_victory
