#spain commie election 1
country_event = {
	id = spain_celections.1
	title = spain_celections.1.t

	desc = { #doesn't have Valencia or Galicia
		text = spain_celections.1.d1
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				owns_state = 171
			}
			NOT = {
				owns_state = 167
			}
		}
	}
	desc = { #has Galicia but not Valencia
		text = spain_celections.1.d2
		trigger = {
			owns_state = 171
			NOT = {
				owns_state = 167
			}
		}
	}
	desc = { #has Valencia but not Galicia
		text = spain_celections.1.d3
		trigger = {
			owns_state = 167
			NOT = {
				owns_state = 171
			}
		}
	}
	desc = { #has Valencia and Galicia
		text = spain_celections.1.d4
		trigger = {
			AND = {
				owns_state = 171
				owns_state = 167
			}
		}
	}

	picture = spr_communist_elections

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #keep centella
		name = spain_celections.1.o1
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = spain_celections.2
				days = 1461
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #monica garcia gomez
		name = spain_celections.1.o2
		IF = {
			limit = { tag = SPR }
			create_country_leader = {
				 name = "Mónica García Gómez"
				 picture = Portrait__SPR_Monica_Garcia.dds
				 ideology = neocommunist
			}
		}
		IF = {
			limit = { tag = SPN }
			create_country_leader = {
				 name = "Mónica García Gómez"
				 picture = Portrait__SPN_Monica_Garcia.dds
				 ideology = neocommunist
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = spain_celections.3
				days = 1461
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #yolanda diaz
		name = spain_celections.1.o3
		trigger = {
			owns_state = 171
		}
		IF = {
			limit = { tag = SPR }
			create_country_leader = {
				 name = "Yolanda Diaz"
				 picture = Portrait_SPR_Yolanda_Diaz.dds
				 ideology = neocommunist
			}
		}
		IF = {
			limit = { tag = SPN }
			create_country_leader = {
				 name = "Yolanda Diaz"
				 picture = Portrait_SPN_Yolanda_Diaz.dds
				 ideology = neocommunist
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = spain_celections.4
				days = 1461
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #joan ribo
		name = spain_celections.1.o4
		trigger = {
			owns_state = 167
		}
		IF = {
			limit = { tag = SPR }
			create_country_leader = {
				 name = "Joan Ribó"
				 picture = Portrait__SPR_Joan_Ribo.dds
				 ideology = neocommunist
			}
		}
		IF = {
			limit = { tag = SPN }
			create_country_leader = {
				 name = "Joan Ribó"
				 picture = Portrait__SPN_Joan_Ribo.dds
				 ideology = neocommunist
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = spain_celections.5
				days = 1461
			}
		}
	}
}

#frutos dies
country_event = {
	id = spain_celections.6
	title = spain_celections.6.t
	desc = spain_celections.6.d
	picture = spr_frutos_fucking_dies

	trigger = {
		has_completed_focus = stalinist_committee_elects_frutos
		has_government = communist
		date > 2020.6.6
	}
	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 30
	}

	option = { #astor garcia
		name = spain_celections.6.o1
		kill_country_leader = yes
		IF = {
			limit = { tag = SPR }
			create_country_leader = {
				 name = "Ástor García"
				 picture = Portrait__SPR_Astor_Garcia.dds
				 ideology = stalinist
			}
		}
		IF = {
			limit = { tag = SPN }
			create_country_leader = {
				 name = "Ástor García"
				 picture = Portrait__SPN_Astor_Garcia.dds
				 ideology = stalinist
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							OR = {
								tag = SPR
								tag = SPN
							}
						}
					}
					news_event = {
						id = spain_news.36
					}
				}
		}
	}
	option = { #robert vaquero
		name = spain_celections.6.o2
		kill_country_leader = yes
		IF = {
			limit = { tag = SPR }
			create_country_leader = {
				 name = "Roberto Vaquero"
				 picture = Portrait_SPR_Roberto_Vaquero.dds
				 ideology = stalinist
			}
		}
		IF = {
			limit = { tag = SPN }
			create_country_leader = {
				 name = "Roberto Vaquero"
				 picture = Portrait_SPN_Roberto_Vaquero.dds
				 ideology = stalinist
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
				every_country = {
					limit = {
						NOT = {
							OR = {
								tag = SPR
								tag = SPN
							}
						}
					}
					news_event = {
						id = spain_news.37
					}
				}
		}
	}

#syndicalist election 1
country_event = {
	id = spain_celections.7
	title = spain_celections.7.t
	desc = spain_celections.7.d
	picture = spr_intersyndical_elections

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #keep the UGT
		name = spain_celections.7.o1
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = spain_celections.8
				days = 1461
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #CNT
		name = spain_celections.7.o2
		IF = {
			limit = { tag = SPR }
			create_country_leader = {
				 name = "The National Confederation of Labor"
				 picture = Portrait__SPR_CNT.dds
				 ideology = anarcho_syndicalism
			}
		}
		IF = {
			limit = { tag = SPN }
			create_country_leader = {
				 name = "The National Confederation of Labor"
				 picture = Portrait__SPN_CNT.dds
				 ideology = anarcho_syndicalism
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = spain_celections.9
				days = 1461
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #CCOO
		name = spain_celections.7.o3
		IF = {
			limit = { tag = SPR }
			create_country_leader = {
				 name = "The Workers' Commissions"
				 picture = Portrait__SPR_CCOO.dds
				 ideology = orthodox_leninist
			}
		}
		IF = {
			limit = { tag = SPN }
			create_country_leader = {
				 name = "The Workers' Commissions"
				 picture = Portrait__SPN_CCOO.dds
				 ideology = orthodox_leninist
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = spain_celections.10
				days = 1461
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #USO
		name = spain_celections.7.o4
		IF = {
			limit = { tag = SPR }
			create_country_leader = {
				 name = "The United Labor Syndicate"
				 picture = Portrait__SPR_USO.dds
				 ideology = christian_communism
			}
		}
		IF = {
			limit = { tag = SPN }
			create_country_leader = {
				 name = "The United Labor Syndicate"
				 picture = Portrait__SPN_USO.dds
				 ideology = christian_communism
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = spain_celections.11
				days = 1461
			}
		}
	}
}

			}

			}
		}
